package io.vertigo.studio.domain.security


create DtDefinition DtRecord {
	stereotype : "KeyConcept"
	id	  dosId			{domain: DoId 		label: "Id"}
	
	field regId 		{domain: DoId 		label: "Region" 		cardinality:"?" }
  	field depId 		{domain: DoId 		label: "Departement" 	cardinality:"?" }
  	field comId 		{domain: DoId 		label: "Commune" 		cardinality:"?" }
  
  	field typId 		{domain: DoId 		label: "Record type" 	cardinality:"1"}
	field title 		{domain: DoString 	label: "Title" 			cardinality:"1"}
	field amount 		{domain: DoConso 	label: "Amount" 		cardinality:"1"}
	field utiIdOwner 	{domain: DoId 		label: "Owner" 			cardinality:"1" }
  
  	field etaCd 		{domain: DoString 	label: "State" 			cardinality:"1"}	
}
